🏆 Tournament Outlook — Progression, Title Odds & Outright Value
Based on 20,000 full-tournament simulations: group stage (host advantage applied) → R32 → R16 → QF → SF → Final. Knockout ties resolved by simulated extra time then a near-even shootout. The R32 bracket is a fixed model bracket (winners spread across the draw, no same-group R32 rematches) — not FIFA’s exact third-place combination table — so individual paths carry some bracket uncertainty; contender title odds are robust to it.
Mkt champ = vig-stripped outright probability from real June 2026 market odds (FOX / FanDuel / ESPN round-ups). Edge = model − market: ◆ model-rich (≥3pp over) / ▽ model-poor (≥3pp under). Big gaps usually reflect the model leaning on recent goal stats while the market weights reputation — France and Spain read model-poor, Argentina and Netherlands model-rich. Treat as directional, not a green light.
